47→\n    48→template <class Base> class FactoryRegistryProxyImpl : public FactoryRegistryProxy {\n    49→public:\n    50→  using FactoryRegistry = Envoy::Registry::FactoryRegistry<Base>;\n    51→\n This enforces correct use of the registration machinery.\n   132→  template <class T, class Base> friend class RegisterFactory;\n   133→  template <class Base> friend class InjectFactoryCategory;\n   134→\n   135→  static void registerCategory(const std::string& category, FactoryRegistryProxy* factory_names) {\n   136→    auto result = factories().emplace(std::make_pair(category, factory_names));\n   137→    RELEASE_ASSERT(result.second == true,\n   138→                   fmt::format(\"Double registration for category: '{}'\", category));\n   139→  }\n   140→\n   141→  static void deregisterCategoryForTest(const std::string& category) {\n   142→    factories().erase(category);\n   143→    RELEASE_ASSERT(factories().find(category) == factories().end(),\n   144→                   fmt::format(\"Deregistration for category '{}' failed\", category));\n   145→  }\n   146→};\n   147→\n   148→// Forward declaration of test class for friend declaration below.\n   149→template <typename T> class InjectFactory;\n   150→\n   151→/**\n   152→ * General registry for implementation factories. The registry is templated by the Base class that a\n   153→ * set of factories conforms to.\n   154→ *\n   155→ * Classes are found by name, so a single name cannot be registered twice for the same Base class.\n   156→ * Factories are registered by reference and this reference is expected to be valid through the life\n   157→ * of the program. Factories cannot be deregistered.\n   158→ * Factories should generally be registered by statically instantiating the RegisterFactory class.\n   159→ *\n   160→ * Note: This class is not thread safe, so registration should only occur in a single threaded\n   161→ * environment, which is guaranteed by the static instantiation mentioned above.\n   162→ *\n   163→ * Example lookup: BaseFactoryType *factory =\n   164→ * FactoryRegistry<BaseFactoryType>::getFactory(\"example_factory_name\");\n   165→ */\n   166→template <class Base> class FactoryRegistry : public Logger::Loggable<Logger::Id::config> {\n   167→public:\n   168→  /**\n   169→   * Return a sorted vector of registered factory names.\n   170→   */\n   171→  static std::vector<absl::string_view> registeredNames(bool include_disabled = false) {\n   172→    std::vector<absl::string_view> ret;\n   173→\n   174→    ret.reserve(factories().size());\n   175→\n   176→    for (const auto& [factory_name, factory] : factories()) {\n   177→      if (factory || include_disabled) {\n   178→        ret.push_back(factory_name);\n   179→      }\n   180→    }\n   181→\n   182→    std::sort(ret.begin(), ret.end());\n   183→\n   184→    return ret;\n   185→  }\n   186→\n   187→  /**\n   188→   * Gets the current map of factory implementations.\n   189→   */\n   190→  static absl::flat_hash_map<std::string, Base*>& factories() {\n   191→    static auto* factories = new absl::flat_hash_map<std::string, Base*>;\n   192→    return *factories;\n   193→  }\n   194→\n   195→  /**\n   196→   * Gets the current map of vendor specific factory versions.\n   197→   */\n   198→  static absl::flat_hash_map<std::string, envoy::config::core::v3::BuildVersion>&\n   199→  versionedFactories() {\n   200→    using VersionedFactoryMap =\n   201→        absl::flat_hash_map<std::string, envoy::config::core::v3::BuildVersion>;\n   202→    MUTABLE_CONSTRUCT_ON_FIRST_USE(VersionedFactoryMap);\n   203→  }\n   204→\n   205→  static absl::flat_hash_map<std::string, std::string>& deprecatedFactoryNames() {\n   206→    static auto* deprecated_factory_names = new absl::flat_hash_map<std::string, std::string>;\n   207→    return *deprecated_factory_names;\n   208→  }\n   209→\n   210→  /**\n   211→   * Lazily constructs a mapping from the configuration message type to a factory,\n   212→   * including the deprecated configuration message types.\n   213→   * Must be invoked after factory registration is completed.\n   214→   */\n   215→  static absl::flat_hash_map<std::string, Base*>& factoriesByType() {\n   216→    static absl::flat_hash_map<std::string, Base*>* factories_by_type =\n   217→        buildFactoriesByType().release();\n   218→\n   219→    return *factories_by_type;\n   220→  }\n   221→\n   222→  static bool& allowDuplicates() {\n   223→    static bool* allow_duplicates = new bool(false);\n   224→    return *allow_duplicates;\n   225→  }\n   226→\n   227→  /**\n   228→   * instead_value are used when passed name was deprecated.\n   229→   */\n   230→  static void registerFactory(Base& factory, absl::string_view name,\n   231→                              absl::string_view instead_value = \"\") {\n   232→    auto result = factories().emplace(std::make_pair(name, &factory));\n   233→    if (!result.second && !allowDuplicates()) {\n   234→      ExceptionUtil::throwEnvoyException(\n   235→          fmt::format(\"Double registration for name: '{}'\", factory.name()));\n   236→    }\n   237→\n   238→    if (!instead_value.empty()) {\n   239→      deprecatedFactoryNames().emplace(std::make_pair(name, instead_value));\n   240→    }\n   241→  }\n   242→\n   243→  /**\n   244→   * version is used for registering vendor specific factories that are versioned\n   245→   * independently of Envoy.\n   246→   */\n   247→  static void registerFactory(Base& factory, absl::string_view name,\n   248→                              const envoy::config::core::v3::BuildVersion& version,\n   249→                              absl::string_view instead_value = \"\") {\n   250→    auto result = factories().emplace(std::make_pair(name, &factory));\n   251→    if (!result.second) {\n   252→      ExceptionUtil::throwEnvoyException(\n   253→          fmt::format(\"Double registration for name: '{}'\", factory.name()));\n   254→    }\n   255→    versionedFactories().emplace(std::make_pair(name, version));\n   256→    if (!instead_value.empty()) {\n   257→      deprecatedFactoryNames().emplace(std::make_pair(name, instead_value));\n   258→    }\n   259→  }\n   260→\n   261→  /**\n   262→   * Permanently disables the named factory by setting the corresponding\n   263→   * factory pointer to null. If the factory is registered under multiple\n   264→   * (deprecated) names, all the possible names are disabled.\n   265→   */\n   266→  static bool disableFactory(absl::string_view name) {\n   267→    const auto disable = [](absl::string_view name) -> bool {\n   268→      auto it = factories().find(name);\n   269→      if (it != factories().end()) {\n   270→        it->second = nullptr;\n   271→        return true;\n   272→      }\n   273→      return false;\n   274→    };\n   275→\n   276→    // First, find the canonical name for this factory.\n   277→    absl::string_view canonicalName = canonicalFactoryName(name);\n   278→\n   279→    // Next, disable the factory by all its deprecated names.\n   280→    for (const auto& [deprecated_name, mapped_canonical_name] : deprecatedFactoryNames()) {\n   281→      if (mapped_canonical_name == canonicalName) {\n   282→        disable(deprecated_name);\n   283→      }\n   284→    }\n   285→\n   286→    // Finally, disable the factory by its canonical name.\n   287→    return disable(canonicalName);\n   288→  }\n   289→\n   290→  /**\n   291→   * Gets a factory by name. If the name isn't found in the registry, returns nullptr.\n   292→   */\n   293→  static Base* getFactory(absl::string_view name) {\n   294→    auto it = factories().find(name);\n   295→    if (it == factories().end()) {\n   296→      return nullptr;\n   297→    }\n   298→\n   299→    return it->second;\n   300→  }\n   301→\n   302→  static Base* getFactoryByType(absl::string_view type) {\n   303→    auto it = factoriesByType().find(type);\n   304→    if (it == factoriesByType().end()) {\n   305→      return nullptr;\n   306→    }\n   307→    return it->second;\n   308→  }\n   309→\n   310→  /**\n   311→   * @return the canonical name of the factory. If the given name is a\n   312→   * deprecated factory name, the canonical name is returned instead.\n   313→   */\n   314→  static absl::string_view canonicalFactoryName(absl::string_view name) {\n   315→    const auto it = deprecatedFactoryNames().find(name);\n   316→    return (it == deprecatedFactoryNames().end()) ? name : it->second;\n   317→  }\n   318→\n   319→  /**\n   320→   * @return true if the named factory was disabled.\n   321→   */\n   322→  static bool isFactoryDisabled(absl::string_view name) {\n   323→    auto it = factories().find(name);\n   324→    ASSERT(it != factories().end());\n   325→    return it->second == nullptr;\n   326→  }\n   327→\n   328→  /**\n   329→   * @return vendor specific version of a factory.\n   330→   */\n   331→  static absl::optional<envoy::config::core::v3::BuildVersion>\n   332→  getFactoryVersion(absl::string_view name) {\n   333→    auto it = versionedFactories().find(name);\n   334→    if (it == versionedFactories().end()) {\n   335→      return absl::nullopt;\n   336→    }\n   337→    return it->second;\n   338→  }\n   339→\n   340→  /**\n   341→   * @return set of config type names indexed by the factory name.\n   342→   */\n   343→  static absl::flat_hash_map<std::string, std::vector<std::string>> registeredTypes() {\n   344→    absl::flat_hash_map<std::string, std::vector<std::string>> mapping;\n   345→    for (const auto& [config_type, factory] : factoriesByType()) {\n   346→      mapping[factory->name()].push_back(config_type);\n   347→    }\n   348→    return mapping;\n   349→  }\n   350→\n   351→private:\n   352→  // Allow factory injection only in tests.\n   353→  friend class InjectFactory<Base>;\n   354→\n   355→  static std::unique_ptr<absl::flat_hash_map<std::string, Base*>> buildFactoriesByType() {\n   356→    auto mapping = std::make_unique<absl::flat_hash_map<std::string, Base*>>();\n   357→\n   358→    for (const auto& [factory_name, factory] : factories()) {\n   359→      UNREFERENCED_PARAMETER(factory_name);\n   360→      if (factory == nullptr) {\n   361→        continue;\n   362→      }\n   363→\n   364→      for (const auto& config_type : factory->configTypes()) {\n   365→        ASSERT(!config_type.empty(), \"Extension config types can never be empty string\");\n   366→\n   367→        // Register config types in the mapping.\n   368→        auto it = mapping->find(config_type);\n   369→        if (it != mapping->end() && it->second != factory) {\n   370→          // Mark double-registered types with a nullptr for tests only.\n   371→          // See issue https://github.com/envoyproxy/envoy/issues/9643.\n   372→          RELEASE_ASSERT(false, fmt::format(\"Double registration for type: '{}' by '{}' and '{}'\",\n   373→                                            config_type, factory->name(),\n   374→                                            it->second ? it->second->name() : \"\"));\n   375→          it->second = nullptr;\n   376→        } else {\n   377→          mapping->emplace(std::make_pair(config_type, factory));\n   378→        }\n   379→      }\n   380→    }\n   381→\n   382→    return mapping;\n   383→  }\n   384→\n   385→  // Rebuild the factories-by-type map based on the current factories.\n   386→  static void rebuildFactoriesByTypeForTest() {\n   387→    auto& mapping = factoriesByType();\n   388→    auto updated_mapping = buildFactoriesByType();\n   389→\n   390→    // Copy the updated mapping over the old one.\n   391→    mapping = *updated_mapping;\n   392→  }\n   393→\n   394→  /**\n   395→   * Replaces a factory by name. This method should only be used for testing purposes.\n   396→   * @param factory is the factory to inject.\n   397→   * @param deprecated_names install the given deprecated names for this factory.\n   398→   * @return std::function<void()> a function that will restore the previously registered factories\n   399→   *         (by name or type).\n   400→   */\n   401→  static std::function<void()>\n   402→  replaceFactoryForTest(Base& factory,\n   403→                        std::initializer_list<absl::string_view> deprecated_names = {}) {\n   404→    using DeprecatedNamesVector = std::vector<std::pair<std::string, std::string>>;\n   405→\n   406→    // If an existing factory is registered with this name, track it for later restoration.\n   407→    Base* prev_by_name = nullptr;\n   408→    auto it = factories().find(factory.name());\n   409→    if (it != factories().end()) {\n   410→      prev_by_name = it->second;\n   411→      factories().erase(it);\n   412→\n   413→      ENVOY_LOG(\n   414→          info, \"Factory '{}' (type '{}') displaced-by-name with test factory '{}' (type '{}')\",\n   415→          prev_by_name->name(), prev_by_name->configTypes(), factory.name(), factory.configTypes());\n   416→    } else {\n   417→      ENVOY_LOG(info, \"Factory '{}' (type '{}') registered for tests\", factory.name(),\n   418→                factory.configTypes());\n   419→    }\n   420→\n   421→    factories().emplace(factory.name(), &factory);\n   422→    RELEASE_ASSERT(getFactory(factory.name()) == &factory,\n   423→                   \"test factory by-name registration failed\");\n   424→\n   425→    DeprecatedNamesVector prev_deprecated_names;\n   426→    if (deprecated_names.size() > 0) {\n   427→      for (auto deprecated_name : deprecated_names) {\n   428→        auto it = deprecatedFactoryNames().find(deprecated_name);\n   429→        if (it != deprecatedFactoryNames().end()) {\n   430→          prev_deprecated_names.emplace_back(std::make_pair(it->first, it->second));\n   431→          deprecatedFactoryNames().erase(it);\n   432→\n   433→          ENVOY_LOG(\n   434→              info,\n   435→              \"Deprecated name '{}' (mapped to '{}') displaced with test factory '{}' (type '{}')\",\n   436→              it->first, it->second, factory.name(), factory.configTypes());\n   437→        } else {\n   438→          // Name not previously mapped, remember to remove it.\n   439→          prev_deprecated_names.emplace_back(std::make_pair(deprecated_name, \"\"));\n   440→\n   441→          ENVOY_LOG(info, \"Deprecated name '{}' (mapped to '{}')\", deprecated_name, factory.name());\n   442→        }\n   443→\n   444→        // Register the replacement factory with a deprecated name.\n   445→        factories().emplace(deprecated_name, &factory);\n   446→        RELEASE_ASSERT(getFactory(deprecated_name) == &factory,\n   447→                       \"test factory registration by deprecated name failed\");\n   448→\n   449→        // Register the replacement factory's deprecated name.\n   450→        deprecatedFactoryNames().emplace(std::make_pair(deprecated_name, factory.name()));\n   451→      }\n   452→    }\n   453→\n   454→    rebuildFactoriesByTypeForTest();\n   455→\n   456→    return [replacement = &factory, prev_by_name, prev_deprecated_names]() {\n   457→      // Unregister the replacement factory by name.\n   458→      factories().erase(replacement->name());\n   459→\n   460→      ENVOY_LOG(info, \"Removed test factory '{}' (type '{}')\", replacement->name(),\n   461→                replacement->configTypes());\n   462→\n   463→      if (prev_by_name) {\n   464→        // Restore any factory displaced by name, but only register the type if it's non-empty.\n   465→        factories().emplace(prev_by_name->name(), prev_by_name);\n   466→\n   467→        ENVOY_LOG(info, \"Restored factory '{}' (type '{}'), formerly displaced-by-name\",\n   468→                  prev_by_name->name(), prev_by_name->configTypes());\n   469→      }\n   470→\n   471→      for (auto [prev_deprecated_name, mapped_canonical_name] : prev_deprecated_names) {\n   472→        deprecatedFactoryNames().erase(prev_deprecated_name);\n   473→\n   474→        ENVOY_LOG(info, \"Removed deprecated name '{}'\", prev_deprecated_name);\n   475→\n   476→        if (!mapped_canonical_name.empty()) {\n   477→          deprecatedFactoryNames().emplace(\n   478→              std::make_pair(prev_deprecated_name, mapped_canonical_name));\n   479→\n   480→          auto* deprecated_factory = getFactory(mapped_canonical_name);\n   481→          RELEASE_ASSERT(deprecated_factory != nullptr,\n   482→                         \"failed to restore deprecated factory name\");\n   483→          factories().emplace(mapped_canonical_name, deprecated_factory);\n   484→\n   485→          ENVOY_LOG(info, \"Restored deprecated name '{}' (mapped to '{}'\", prev_deprecated_name,\n   486→                    mapped_canonical_name);\n   487→        }\n   488→      }\n   489→\n   490→      rebuildFactoriesByTypeForTest();\n   491→    };\n   492→  }\n   493→};\n   494→\n   495→/**\n   496→ * Factory registration template. Enables users to register a particular implementation factory with\n   497→ * the FactoryRegistry by instantiating this templated class with the specific factory class and the\n   498→ * general Base class to which that factory conforms.\n   499→ *\n   500→ * Because factories are generally registered once and live for the length of the program, the\n   501→ * standard use of this class is static instantiation within a linked implementation's translation\n   502→ * unit. For an example of a typical use case, @see NamedNetworkFilterConfigFactory.\n   503→ *\n   504→ * Example registration: REGISTER_FACTORY(SpecificFactory, BaseFactory);\n   505→ *                       LEGACY_REGISTER_FACTORY(SpecificFactory, BaseFactory, \"deprecated_name\");\n   506→ */\n   507→template <class T, class Base> class RegisterFactory {\n   508→public:\n   509→  /**\n   510→   * Constructor that registers an instance of the factory with the FactoryRegistry.\n   511→   */\n   512→  RegisterFactory() {\n   513→    ASSERT(!instance_.name().empty());\n   514→    FactoryRegistry<Base>::registerFactory(instance_, instance_.name());\n   515→\n   516→    // Also register this factory with its category.\n   517→    //\n   518→    // Each time a factory registers, the registry will attempt to\n   519→    // register its category here. This means that we have to ignore\n   520→    // multiple attempts to register the same category and can't detect\n   521→    // duplicate categories.\n   522→    if (!FactoryCategoryRegistry::isRegistered(instance_.category())) {\n   523→      FactoryCategoryRegistry::registerCategory(instance_.category(),\n   524→                                                new FactoryRegistryProxyImpl<Base>());\n   525→    }\n   526→  }\n   527→\n   528→  /**\n   529→   * Constructor that registers an instance of the factory with the FactoryRegistry along with\n   530→   * deprecated names.\n   531→   */\n   532→  explicit RegisterFactory(std::initializer_list<absl::string_view> deprecated_names) {\n   533→    if (!instance_.name().empty()) {\n   534→      FactoryRegistry<Base>::registerFactory(instance_, instance_.name());\n   535→    } else {\n   536→      ASSERT(deprecated_names.size() != 0,\n   537→             \"Attempted to register a factory without a name or deprecated name\");\n   538→    }\n   539→\n   540→    for (auto deprecated_name : deprecated_names) {\n   541→      ASSERT(!deprecated_name.empty());\n   542→      FactoryRegistry<Base>::registerFactory(instance_, deprecated_name, instance_.name());\n   543→    }\n   544→\n   545→    if (!FactoryCategoryRegistry::isRegistered(instance_.category())) {\n   546→      FactoryCategoryRegistry::registerCategory(instance_.category(),\n   547→                                                new FactoryRegistryProxyImpl<Base>());\n   548→    }\n   549→  }\n   550→\n   551→  /**\n   552→   * Constructor that registers an instance of the factory with the FactoryRegistry along with\n   553→   * vendor specific version.\n   554→   */\n   555→  RegisterFactory(uint32_t major, uint32_t minor, uint32_t patch,\n   556→                  const std::map<std::string, std::string>& version_metadata)\n   557→      : RegisterFactory(major, minor, patch, version_metadata, {}) {}\n   558→\n   559→  /**\n   560→   * Constructor that registers an instance of the factory with the FactoryRegistry along with\n   561→   * vendor specific version and deprecated names.\n   562→   */\n   563→  RegisterFactory(uint32_t major, uint32_t minor, uint32_t patch,\n   564→                  const std::map<std::string, std::string>& version_metadata,\n   565→                  std::initializer_list<absl::string_view> deprecated_names) {\n   566→    auto version = makeBuildVersion(major, minor, patch, version_metadata);\n   567→    if (instance_.name().empty()) {\n   568→      ASSERT(deprecated_names.size() != 0);\n   569→    } else {\n   570→      FactoryRegistry<Base>::registerFactory(instance_, instance_.name(), version);\n   571→    }\n   572→\n   573→    for (auto deprecated_name : deprecated_names) {\n   574→      ASSERT(!deprecated_name.empty());\n   575→      FactoryRegistry<Base>::registerFactory(instance_, deprecated_name, version, instance_.name());\n   576→    }\n   577→\n   578→    if (!FactoryCategoryRegistry::isRegistered(instance_.category())) {\n   579→      FactoryCategoryRegistry::registerCategory(instance_.category(),\n   580→                                                new FactoryRegistryProxyImpl<Base>());\n   581→    }\n   582→  }\n   583→\n   584→private:\n   585→  static envoy::config::core::v3::BuildVersion\n   586→  makeBuildVersion(uint32_t major, uint32_t minor, uint32_t patch,\n   587→                   const std::map<std::string, std::string>& metadata) {\n   588→    envoy::config::core::v3::BuildVersion version;\n   589→    version.mutable_version()->set_major_number(major);\n   590→    version.mutable_version()->set_minor_number(minor);\n   591→    version.mutable_version()->set_patch(patch);\n   592→    *version.mutable_metadata() = MessageUtil::keyValueStruct(metadata);\n   593→    return version;\n   594→  }\n   595→\n   596→  T instance_{};\n   597→};\n   598→\n   599→/**\n   600→ * RegisterInternalFactory is a special case for registering factories\n   601→ * that are considered internal implementation details that should\n   602→ * not be exposed to operators via the factory categories.\n   603→ *\n   604→ * There is no corresponding REGISTER_INTERNAL_FACTORY because\n   605→ * this should be used sparingly and only in special cases.\n   606→ */\n   607→template <class T, class Base> class RegisterInternalFactory {\n   608→public:\n   609→  RegisterInternalFactory() {\n   610→    ASSERT(!instance_.name().empty());\n   611→    FactoryRegistry<Base>::registerFactory(instance_, instance_.name());\n   612→  }\n   613→\n   614→private:\n   615→  T instance_{};\n   616→};\n   617→\n   618→#ifdef   for (const auto& [factory_name, factory] : factories()) {\n      UNREFERENCED_PARAMETER(factory_name);\n      if (factory == nullptr) {\n        continue;\n      }\n\n      for (const auto&            factory.configTypes());\n    }\n\n    factories().emplace(factory.name(), &factory);\n    RELEASE_ASSERT(getFactory(factory.name()) == &factory,\n                   \"test factory by-name Envoyproxy/Envoy:\\n\\n## Factory Registration System\\n\\nThe filter factory registry is implemented in `envoy/registry/registry.h`, which provides a template-based generic registry pattern:\\n- `FactoryRegistry<Base>` maintains a global map of factory instances indexed by name\\n- `RegisterFactory<T, Base>` enables static registration of filter factory implementations\\n- The `REGISTER_FACTORY` and `LEGACY_REGISTER_FACTORY` macros (defined in registry.h) are used throughout the codebase to register filters\\n\\n## HTTP Filter Factory Interface\\n\\nThe `NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory` interface is defined in `envoy/server/filter_config.h`. Each HTTP filter must implement this interface with a factory name. The key method is:\\n- `createFilterFactoryFromProto()` - creates an `Http::FilterFactoryCb` from protobuf configuration\\n\\nThe `Http::FilterFactoryCb` is a callback function type (defined in `envoy/http/filter_factory.h`) that takes `FilterChainFactoryCallbacks&` and creates filter instances for each request.\\n\\n## Filter Chain Creation Flow\\n\\n**Configuration Time (startup):**\\n1. `HttpConnectionManagerConfig` in `source/extensions/filters/network/http_connection_manager/config.h` implements `Http::FilterChainFactory`\\n2. `FilterChainHelper` in `source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h` processes the filter configuration from the protobuf\\n3. `FilterChainHelper::processFilter()` looks up the filter factory from the registry and calls `createFilterFactoryFromProto()` to get the `FilterFactoryCb`\\n4. These callbacks are stored in `filter_factories_` for later use\\n\\n**Per-Request Instantiation (runtime):**\\n1. This calls `HttpConnectionManagerConfig::createFilterChain()` which calls `FilterChainUtility::createFilterChainForFactories()` (in `source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.cc`)\\n4. For each stored `FilterFactoryCb`, it calls `FilterManager::applyFilterFactoryCb()`\\n5. `applyFilterFactoryCb()` creates a `FilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl` and invokes the `FilterFactoryCb` with it\\n\\n## Per-Request Filter Instantiation\\n\\nThe `FilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl` class (defined in `source/common/http/filter_manager.h`) implements the `FilterChainFactoryCallbacks` interface and handles the actual filter instantiation:\\n\\n- `addStreamDecoderFilter()` - creates an `ActiveStreamDecoderFilter` wrapper around the filter instance and adds it to the decoder filter chain\\n- `addStreamEncoderFilter()` - creates an `ActiveStreamEncoderFilter` wrapper and adds it to the encoder filter chain\\n- `addStreamFilter()` - creates both wrapper types for bidirectional filters\\n\\nThe `ActiveStreamDecoderFilter` and `ActiveStreamEncoderFilter` wrappers (defined in `source/common/http/filter_manager.h`) manage the filter lifecycle, handle iteration state, and invoke the actual filter methods.\\n\\n## Concrete Example\\n\\nThe Router filter implementation in `source/extensions/filters/http/router/config.cc` demonstrates the pattern:\\n- `RouterFilterConfig` inherits from `FactoryBase<...>` (defined in `source/extensions/filters/http/common/factory_base.h`)\\n- `createFilterFactoryFromProtoTyped()` returns a lambda function that is the `FilterFactoryCb`\\n- This lambda captures the filter configuration and, when called during filter chain creation, uses `callbacks.addStreamDecoderFilter()` to instantiate a `Router::ProdFilter` for the current request\\n- The filter is registered via `LEGACY_REGISTER_FACTORY` macro, adding it to the global factory registry\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":5,"cache_creation_input_tokens":7328,"cache_read_input_tokens":76203,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":7328},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"05f21d90-f6bb-4a9e-a100-4d6e01e16fb1","uuid":"2690723c-ce5e-4abf-9bf8-a956c8f49858"}

For each stored `FilterFactoryCb`, it calls `FilterManager::applyFilterFactoryCb()`\\n5. `applyFilterFactoryCb()` creates a `FilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl` and invokes the `FilterFactoryCb` with it\\n\\n## Per-Request Filter Instantiation\\n\\nThe `FilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl` class (defined in `source/common/http/filter_manager.h`) implements the `FilterChainFactoryCallbacks` interface and handles the actual filter instantiation:\\n\\n- `addStreamDecoderFilter()` - creates an `ActiveStreamDecoderFilter` wrapper around the filter instance and adds it to the decoder filter chain\\n- `addStreamEncoderFilter()` - creates an `ActiveStreamEncoderFilter` wrapper and adds it to the encoder filter chain\\n- `addStreamFilter()` - creates both wrapper types for bidirectional filters\\n\\nThe `ActiveStreamDecoderFilter` and `ActiveStreamEncoderFilter` wrappers (defined in `source/common/http/filter_manager.h`) manage the filter lifecycle, handle iteration state, and invoke the actual filter methods.\\n\\n## Concrete Example\\n\\nThe Router filter implementation in `source/extensions/filters/http/router/config.cc` demonstrates the pattern:\\n- `RouterFilterConfig` inherits from `FactoryBase<...>` (defined in `source/extensions/filters/http/common/factory_base.h`)\\n- `createFilterFactoryFromProtoTyped()` returns a lambda function that is the `FilterFactoryCb`\\n- This lambda captures the filter configuration and, when called during filter chain creation, uses `callbacks.addStreamDecoderFilter()` to instantiate a `Router::ProdFilter` for the current request\\n- The filter is registered via `LEGACY_REGISTER_FACTORY` macro, adding it to the global factory registry\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
